data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0"><h1 class="article-title" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.0">Trinidad and Tobago 0, USA 0 | CONCACAF World Cup Qualifier Match Recap</h1><div class="byline" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1"><address class="author" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0"><a data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0.0" href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/author/Dan Itel" rel="author">Dan Itel</a></address><time class="pubdate" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.1" datetime="2015-11-18">Nov 18, 2015</time></div><div data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.2"></div><div class="gigya-share" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.4" id="article-share"></div><img class="article-primary-image" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.5" src="http://league-mp7static.mlsdigital.net/styles/image_default/s3/images/USATSI_7980518_167117764_lowres_0.jpg"><article class="article" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.6"><p>The US national team knew they\xe2\x80\x99d have a much tougher fight on their hands Tuesday night in Trinidad &amp;\xc2\xa0Tobago than what they faced in their CONCACAF World Cup qualifying opening <a href="http://matchcenter.mlssoccer.com/matchcenter/2015-11-13-us-mens-national-team-vs-st-vincent-the-grenadines/recap">6-1 win last week over minnows St. Vincent &amp; the Grenadines</a>.</p>\n<p>And they indeed were given all they could handle in a closely contested match that ended in a scoreless draw Tuesday night at Hasely Crawford Stadium in Port of Spain.</p>\n<p>The draw\xc2\xa0leaves the USMNT and Trinidad &amp; Tobago tied atop Group 3 with four points through two matches. Trinidad beat Guatemala 2-1 last week.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><strong><a href="http://matchcenter.mlssoccer.com/matchcenter/2015-11-17-trinidad-and-tobago-vs-us-mens-national-team/boxscore">GET STATS AND LINEUPS FROM THE MATCH</a></strong></li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style="line-height: 1.6em;">Head coach Jurgen Klinsmann made a handful of changes from Friday\xe2\x80\x99s win over St. Vincent &amp; the Grenadines, most notably handing veteran goalkeeper Tim Howard just his second start since he returned from his self-imposed hiatus following\xc2\xa0his heroics against Belgium in the 2014 World Cup.\xc2\xa0</span></p>\n<p>Keeping the flat 4-4-2 formation from Friday, Klinsmann also slid LA Galaxy forward <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/gyasi-zardes">Gyasi Zardes</a> from the right wing up top alongside <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/jozy-altidore">Jozy Altidore</a>, moving Bobby Wood to the bench and DeAndre Yedlin from right back to the wing and Michael Orozco off the bench to right\xc2\xa0back.</p>\n<p>The US backline was\xc2\xa0tested right away when, 20 seconds in, Kenwyne Jones broke free on the right wing for an open cross to the Chicago Fire midfielder\xc2\xa0<a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/joevin-jones">Joevin Jones</a> at the top of the box. Jones sent his right-footed blast well high, however.</p>\n<p>The Soca Warriors had another golden opportunity in the 13th minute when Kenwyne Jones took a long ball at the edge of the area, fended off Orozco, spun and fired just high.</p>\n<p>The USMNT began to pick up steam on the 20-minute mark, when both Fabian Johnson and Altidore fired off shots.\xc2\xa0</p>\n<ul>\n<li><strong><a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/meta/club/united-states">Get more USMNT news and notes from MLSsoccer.com</a></strong></li>\n</ul>\n<p>The Americans rocked onto the front foot in the second half, nearly finding the opener in the 47th minute when Altidore sent a perfect cross across the box to Zardes, who rose up for a booming header that clanged off the bar.</p>\n<p>The US found woodwork again in the 78th minute\xc2\xa0when <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/jermaine-jones">Jermaine Jones</a> took a go from nearly 40 yards out, a right-footed shot that beat goalkeeper Jan Michael-Williams but grazed off the top of the bar.\xc2\xa0</p>\n<p>In the end, even with the offensive\xc2\xa0substitutions\xc2\xa0of Portland Timbers attacker <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/darlington-nagbe">Darlington Nagbe</a> -- making\xc2\xa0his second USMNT appearance in his first camp --\xc2\xa0and Wood, the Yanks were unable to pierce the Soca Warriors&amp;apos; defense.\xc2\xa0</p>\n<p>The USMNT will complete the first round of Group 2 matches when they face Guatemala twice in a home and away during the March 2016 FIFA window.\xc2\xa0</p>\n</article><div class="gigya-comments" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.8" id="article-comments"></div></img></div></div><div class="ad-wrapper" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.1" id="matchcenter-recap-1"></div></div></div></section></div></section></main><div class="connection-warning" data-reactid=".6wogwe8000.a" style="pointer-events:none;">Connection Lost.
